### ๐ก ูฺฉุงุช ู ุชุฑููุฏูุง

```bash
# ูุตุจ Dependencies
npm install

# ุฑุงูโุงูุฏุงุฒ PostgreSQL ุจุง Docker
docker-compose up -d postgres

# ุงุฌุฑุง Migrations
npm run migrate:dev

# ุงุฌุฑุง Bot ุฏุฑ ุญุงูุช Polling (ุจุฑุง Test)
npm run bot

# ุงุฌุฑุง Mini App
npm run dev
```

**2. ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ุงุฒ Environment Files:**

```bash
# .env.example - Template (ุฏุฑ Git)
BOT_TOKEN=your_bot_token_here
BOT_OWNER_ID=your_telegram_id
DATABASE_URL=postgresql://...

# .env - ูุงู ูุงูุน (ุฏุฑ .gitignore)
BOT_TOKEN=1234567890:ABC...
BOT_OWNER_ID=123456789
DATABASE_URL=postgresql://real_connection_string
```

**3. ุชุณุช ูุจู ุงุฒ Deploy:**

ููุดู ุฏุฑ ูุญุท local ุชุณุช ฺฉูุฏ:

```bash
# Build ฺฉุฑุฏู Mini App
npm run build

# ุงฺฏุฑ ุจุฏูู ุฎุทุง build ุดุฏุ ุขูุงุฏู deploy ุงุณุช โ
```

**4. Git Workflow:**

```bash
# Branch ุฌุฏุฏ ุจุฑุง feature
git checkout -b feature/new-feature

# ุชุบุฑุงุช ุฑุง commit ฺฉูุฏ
git add .
git commit -m "feat: add new feature"

# Push ุจู GitHub
git push origin feature/new-feature

# ุจุนุฏ ุงุฒ ุชุณุชุ merge ุจู main
git checkout main
git merge feature/new-feature
git push origin main
```

**5. Script ูุง ููุฏ:**

**Script 1: Backup ุณุฑุน Database:**
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# backup-db.sh
pg_dump "$DATABASE_URL" > "backup_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).sql"
echo "โ Backup created successfully!"
```

**Script 2: Health Check:**
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# health-check.sh
echo "๐ Checking Backend..."
curl -f https://your-backend.onrender.com/healthz || echo "โ Backend is down!"

echo "๐ Checking Mini App..."
curl -f https://your-miniapp.onrender.com || echo "โ Mini App is down!"
```

## ๐ ุจูุชุฑู ุฑูุดโูุง (Best Practices)

### โ ฺุฒูุง ฺฉู ุจุงุฏ ุงูุฌุงู ุฏูุฏ:

1. **Environment Variables ุฑุง ุจู ุฏุฑุณุช ูุฏุฑุช ฺฉูุฏ**
   - ููู Secrets ุฏุฑ Render Dashboard
   - ูุฑฺฏุฒ ุฏุฑ ฺฉุฏ ูุงุฑุฏฺฉุฏ ูฺฉูุฏ

2. **ุงุฒ Git Branches ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ฺฉูุฏ**
   - `main` ุจุฑุง production
   - `develop` ุจุฑุง development
   - Feature branches ุจุฑุง ูฺฺฏโูุง ุฌุฏุฏ

3. **ูุจู ุงุฒ Deploy ุชุณุช ฺฉูุฏ**
   - ุฏุฑ ูุญุท local ุชุณุช ฺฉูุฏ
   - Build ุฑุง ฺฺฉ ฺฉูุฏ
   - Logs ุฑุง ุจุจูุฏ

4. **Backup ููุธู ุจฺฏุฑุฏ**
   - ุฑูุฒุงูู ุงุฒ database
   - ูุจู ุงุฒ ุชุบุฑุงุช ุจุฒุฑฺฏ

5. **Logs ุฑุง ูุฑุชุจุงู ุจุฑุฑุณ ฺฉูุฏ**
   - ูุฑ ฺูุฏ ุฑูุฒ ฺฉโุจุงุฑ
   - ุจุนุฏ ุงุฒ Deploy
   - ููุช ูุดฺฉู ฺฏุฒุงุฑุด ูโุดูุฏ

6. **ูุณุชูุฏุงุช ุจููุณุฏ**
   - ุชุบุฑุงุช ฺฉู ุงูุฌุงู ุฏุงุฏุฏ
   - Environment Variables ุฌุฏุฏ
   - ูฺฉุงุช ููู

### โ ฺุฒูุง ฺฉู ูุจุงุฏ ุงูุฌุงู ุฏูุฏ:

1. **Secrets ุฑุง ุฏุฑ ฺฉุฏ commit ูฺฉูุฏ**
   - โ ูุฑฺฏุฒ `.env` ุฑุง push ูฺฉูุฏ
   - โ TOKEN ูุง ุฑุง ุฏุฑ ฺฉุฏ ูููุณุฏ

2. **ูุณุชููุงู ุฑู branch ุงุตู ุชุบุฑ ูุฏูุฏ**
   - โ ูุณุชูู ุฑู `main` commit ูฺฉูุฏ
   - โ ุงุฒ feature branches ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ฺฉูุฏ

3. **ุจุฏูู ุชุณุช deploy ูฺฉูุฏ**
   - โ ุชุบุฑุงุช ุฑุง ุจุฏูู ุชุณุช push ูฺฉูุฏ
   - โ ููุดู local test ฺฉูุฏ

4. **Database ุฑุง ุจุฏูู backup ุชุบุฑ ูุฏูุฏ**
   - โ Migration ูุง ุฎุทุฑูุงฺฉ ุจุฏูู backup
   - โ ูุจู ุงุฒ ูุฑ ุชุบุฑ backup ุจฺฏุฑุฏ

5. **ุงุฒ Logging ุจโุฑูู ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ูฺฉูุฏ**
   - โ ูุฑ ฺุฒ ุฑุง log ูฺฉูุฏ
   - โ Sensitive data ุฑุง log ูฺฉูุฏ

## ๐ ุจูุชุฑู ุฑูุดโูุง (Best Practices)
